Standard Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
===========================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on June 3, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











Yesterday, Grand Prix Amsterdam competitors had one last chance to earn two byes for the main event by entering the Grand Prix Trials. The winning decklists traditionally give a first impression of what to expect over the course of the weekend. You can find 20 of them below.


Among these 20, Temur Aetherworks Marvel dominated: 10 pilots showed that it's a marvelous world we're living in. But a variety of other archetypes were seen as well. There were two Mardu Vehicles and two White-Blue Flash decks, as well as several one-ofs: Mono Black Zombies, Esper Vehicles, Jeskai Legends, and Blue-Red Emerge.










#### Vlad Croitoru's Mardu Vehicles – GP Amsterdam 2017 Trial Winner


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
